################################################################################################################################################################
#####################################################################Abrocomidae################################################################################
################################################################################################################################################################

#Tree generated based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007) and taxonomy
PHYLO<-read.tree(text="((Cuscomys_ashaninka:1, Cuscomys_oblativa:1):1,Abrocoma_bennettii:1);")
Sister2("Abrocoma_bennettii", "Abrocoma_boliviensis", "Abrocoma_cinerea")
PHYLO<-bind.tree( PHYLO, read.tree(text="(Abrocoma_cinerea:1, Abrocoma_budini:1, Abrocoma_famatina:1, Abrocoma_shistacea:1, Abrocoma_vaccarum:1):1;"),  getNode(phylo4(PHYLO),"Abrocoma_cinerea"))
SisterOrSing1(c("Abrocoma_bennettii", "Abrocoma_boliviensis", "Abrocoma_cinerea", "Abrocoma_budini", "Abrocoma_famatina", "Abrocoma_shistacea", "Abrocoma_vaccarum"),  "Abrocoma_uspallata")

#Simulate potential branch lengths wihtin the family based on a divergence time with its closest relatives of 28.24 MYA following Meredith et al (2011)
#A node called Rootnode_Abrocomidae is temporarily added but will be deleted when the tree is combined with the remaining families in the order
PHYLO<-bind.tree(read.tree(text="(ROOT_1:1, Rootnode_Abrocomidae:1);"), PHYLO,1)
BD.gen(28.24,0.329)
PHYLO->Abrocomidae

################################################################################################################################################################
#####################################################################Anomaluridae###############################################################################
################################################################################################################################################################

#Tree generated based on taxonomy
PHYLO<-read.tree(text="(Zenkerella_insignis:1, AAA:1):0;")
Sister2("Zenkerella_insignis", "Anomalurus_beecrofti", "Idiurus_macrotis")
Sister1("Idiurus_macrotis", "Idiurus_zenkeri")
PHYLO<-bind.tree(PHYLO, read.tree(text="(Anomalurus_beecrofti:1, Anomalurus_derbianus:1, Anomalurus_pelii:1, Anomalurus_pusillus:1):1;"), getNode(phylo4(PHYLO), "Anomalurus_beecrofti")); PHYLO<-drop.tip(PHYLO, "AAA")

#Simulate potential branch lengths wihtin the family based on MRCA of family equal to 40 MYA based on Meredith et al (2011)
BD.gen(40,0.685)
PHYLO->Anomaluridae

#####################################################################Bathyergidae###############################################################################
################################################################################################################################################################

#One of the trees of the family from the posterior distribution
Bathyergidae<-read.tree(text="(Heterocephalus_glaber:1,(Heliophobius_argenteocinereus:1,((Bathyergus_suillus:1,Georychus_capensis:1):1,(((Cryptomys_darlingi:1,(Cryptomys_damarensis:1,(Cryptomys_kafuensis:1,Cryptomys_anselli:1):1):1):1,Cryptomys_mechowi:1):1,Cryptomys_hottentotus:1):1):1):1);")
PHYLO<-Bathyergidae
#One of the trees for the genus Cryptomys from the posterior distribution
Cryptomys<-read.tree(text="((((Cryptomys_mechowi:1,(Cryptomys_foxi:1,Cryptomys_ochraceocinereus:1):1):1,Cryptomys_bocagei:1):1,(Cryptomys_damarensis:1,((Cryptomys_anselli:1,Cryptomys_kafuensis:1):1,Cryptomys_darlingi:1):1):1):1,Cryptomys_hottentotus:1);")
MONOP.GROUP<-c("Cryptomys_anselli", "Cryptomys_bocagei", "Cryptomys_damarensis", "Cryptomys_darlingi", "Cryptomys_foxi", "Cryptomys_hottentotus", "Cryptomys_kafuensis", "Cryptomys_mechowi", "Cryptomys_ochraceocinereus")
#Merging the family tree with the tree for Cryptomys
Replace.groups(Cryptomys, MONOP.GROUP)

#Place Bathyergus_janetta based on taxonomy
Sister1("Bathyergus_suillus", "Bathyergus_janetta")
#Place Cryptomys_zechi based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007)
SisterOrSing1(c("Cryptomys_anselli", "Cryptomys_damarensis", "Cryptomys_mechowi", "Cryptomys_bocagei", "Cryptomys_foxi", "Cryptomys_ochraceocinereus", list(c("Cryptomys_hottentotus", "Cryptomys_darlingi"))), "Cryptomys_zechi")

#Simulate potential branch lengths wihtin the family based on a divergence time with its closest relatives of 28.24 MYA following Meredith et al (2011)
#A node called Rootnode_Bathyergidae is temporarily added but will be deleted when the tree is combined with the remaining families in the order
PHYLO<-bind.tree(read.tree(text="(ROOT_1:1, Rootnode_Bathyergidae:1);"), PHYLO,1)
BD.gen(42.02,0.329)
PHYLO->Bathyergidae

################################################################################################################################################################
##########################################################################Cavidae###############################################################################
################################################################################################################################################################

#One of the trees of the family from the posterior distribution
Cavidae<-read.tree(text="(((Hydrochoerus_hydrochaeris:1,Kerodon_rupestris:1):1,(Dolichotis_salinicola:1,Dolichotis_patagonum:1):1):1,((Microcavia_australis:1,Cavia_aperea:1):1,(Galea_spixii:1,Galea_musteloides:1):1):1);")
PHYLO<-Cavidae
#One of the trees for the genus Cavia from the posterior distribution
Cavia<-read.tree(text="(Cavia_magna:1,(Cavia_tschudii:1,(Cavia_aperea:1,Cavia_fulgida:1):1):1);")
MONOP.GROUP<-c("Cavia_aperea", "Cavia_fulgida", "Cavia_intermedia", "Cavia_magna", "Cavia_tschudii")
#Merging the family tree with the tree for Cavia
Replace.groups(Cavia, MONOP.GROUP)

#Place missing species of Galea based on taxonomy
Rep_2_4("Galea_musteloides", "Galea_spixii", c("Galea_flavidens", "Galea_monasteriensis"))
#Place missing species of Microcavia based on taxonomy
Sister2("Microcavia_australis", "Microcavia_niata", "Microcavia_shiptoni")
#Place Hydrochoerus_isthmius based on taxonomy
Sister1("Hydrochoerus_hydrochaeris", "Hydrochoerus_isthmius")
#Place Kerodon_acrobata based on taxonomy
Sister1("Kerodon_rupestris", "Kerodon_acrobata")
#Place Cavia_intermedia based on taxonomy
SisterOrSing1(c("Cavia_aperea", "Cavia_fulgida", "Cavia_magna", "Cavia_tschudii"), "Cavia_intermedia")
#Place Neochoerus as sister to Hydrochoeris since they belong to the same subfamily
SisterAnd1(c("Hydrochoerus_hydrochaeris", "Hydrochoerus_isthmius"), "Neochoerus_aesopi")

#Simulate potential branch lengths wihtin the family based on MRCA of family equal to 19.94 MYA based on Meredith et al (2011)
BD.gen(19.94,0.329)
PHYLO->Cavidae

Sister2("Alticola_argentatus", "Alticola_lemminus", "Alticola_strelzowi")
TR<-read.tree(text="(Alticola_albicaudus:1,Alticola_argentatus:1,Alticola_barakshin:1,Alticola_macrotis:1,Alticola_montosa:1,Alticola_roylei:1,Alticola_semicanus:1,Alticola_stoliczkanus:1,(Alticola_tuvinicus:1,Alticola_olchonensis:1):1):1;")

TR<-read.tree(text="(Sicista_armenica:1, Sicista_betulina:1, Sicista_caucasica:1, Sicista_caudata:1, Sicista_concolor:1, Sicista_kazbegica:1, Sicista_kluchorica:1, Sicista_napaea:1,  Sicista_pseudonapaea:1, Sicista_severtzovi:1, Sicista_strandi:1, Sicista_subtilis:1, Sicista_tianshanica:1):1;")
PHYLO<<-bind.tree(PHYLO, TR ,  getNode(phylo4(PHYLO),"Sicista_kazbegica"))
#Place Eremodipus and Stylodipus assuming a four way polytomi between Dipus, Eremodipu, Jaculus and Stylodipus
Rep_2_4("Dipus_sagitta", "Jaculus_jaculus", c("Eremodipus_lichtensteini", "Stylodipus_andrewsi"))
Sister2("Stylodipus_andrewsi", "Stylodipus_sungorus", "Stylodipus_telum")
#Place missing species of Jaculus based on taxonomy
Sister2("Jaculus_jaculus", "Jaculus_blanfordi", "Jaculus_orientalis")
#Place Paradipus, Euchoreutes and Salpingotus assuming a deep polyphyly in the family based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007)
Start<-c(list(c("Sicista_armenica", "Sicista_betulina", "Sicista_caucasica", "Sicista_caudata", "Sicista_concolor", "Sicista_kazbegica", "Sicista_kluchorica", "Sicista_napaea",  "Sicista_pseudonapaea", "Sicista_severtzovi", "Sicista_strandi", "Sicista_subtilis", "Sicista_tianshanica")), list(c("Dipus_sagitta", "Jaculus_jaculus", "Jaculus_blanfordi", "Jaculus_orientalis",  "Eremodipus_lichtensteini", "Stylodipus_andrewsi", "Stylodipus_sungorus", "Stylodipus_telum")),list(c("Napaeozapus_insignis", "Eozapus_setchuanus", "Zapus_hudsonius", "Zapus_princeps", "Zapus_trinotatus")))
MIS<-c("Paradipus_ctenodactylus", "Euchoreutes_naso", "Salpingotus_heptneri")
MIS1<-MIS[sample.int(3, 1)]; SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS1); MIS<-MIS[MIS%in%MIS1==F]; Start<-c(Start, MIS1)
MIS1<-MIS[sample.int(2, 1)]; SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS1); MIS<-MIS[MIS%in%MIS1==F]; Start<-c(Start, MIS1)
SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS)
#Place missing species of Salpingotus based on taxonomy
TR<-read.tree(text="(Salpingotus_crassicauda:1, Salpingotus_heptneri:1,Salpingotus_kozlovi:1, Salpingotus_pallidus:1):1;")
PHYLO<<-bind.tree(PHYLO, TR ,  getNode(phylo4(PHYLO),"Salpingotus_heptneri"))

SisterAnd1(c("Salpingotus_crassicauda", "Salpingotus_heptneri", "Salpingotus_kozlovi", "Salpingotus_pallidus"), "Salpingotulus_michaelis")
#Place Cardiocranius as sister to Salpingotulus and Salpingotus based on based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007)
SisterAnd1(c("Salpingotus_crassicauda", "Salpingotus_heptneri", "Salpingotus_kozlovi", "Salpingotus_pallidus", "Salpingotulus_michaelis"), "Cardiocranius_paradoxus")
#Place Allactodipus and Pygeretmus combined as sisters to Sicista, Dipus, Jaculus, Eremodipus, Stylodipus, Napaeozapus, Eozapus, Zapus, Paradipus, Euchoreutes, Cardiocranius, Salpingotulus and Salpingotus based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007) and assumed subfamily monophyly
SisterAnd1(c("Sicista_armenica", "Sicista_betulina", "Sicista_caucasica", "Sicista_caudata", "Sicista_concolor", "Sicista_kazbegica", "Sicista_kluchorica", "Sicista_napaea",  "Sicista_pseudonapaea", "Sicista_severtzovi", "Sicista_strandi", "Sicista_subtilis", "Sicista_tianshanica", "Dipus_sagitta", "Jaculus_jaculus", "Jaculus_blanfordi", "Jaculus_orientalis",  "Eremodipus_lichtensteini", "Stylodipus_andrewsi", "Stylodipus_sungorus", "Stylodipus_telum", "Napaeozapus_insignis", "Eozapus_setchuanus", "Zapus_hudsonius", "Zapus_princeps", "Zapus_trinotatus", "Paradipus_ctenodactylus", "Euchoreutes_naso", "Cardiocranius_paradoxus", "Salpingotulus_michaelis", "Salpingotus_crassicauda", "Salpingotus_heptneri", "Salpingotus_kozlovi", "Salpingotus_pallidus"), "Allactodipus_bobrinskii")
Sister1("Allactodipus_bobrinskii", "Pygeretmus_pumilio")
Sister2("Pygeretmus_pumilio", "Pygeretmus_platyurus", "Pygeretmus_zhitkovi")
#Delete temporary taxon 
PHYLO<-drop.tip(PHYLO, "B")

#Simulate potential branch lengths wihtin the family based on MRCA of family equal to 47 MYA based on Meredith et al (2011)
BD.gen(47,0.685)
PHYLO->Dipodidae

Thomomys<-read.tree(text="((Thomomys_monticola:1,(Thomomys_talpoides:1,Thomomys_mazama:1):1):1,(((Thomomys_bottae:1,Thomomys_umbrinus:1):1,Thomomys_townsendii:1):1,Thomomys_bulbivorus:1):1);")

#Place Pappogeomys_alcorni based on taxonomy
Sister1( "Pappogeomys_bulleri",  "Pappogeomys_alcorni")
#Place missing species of Thomomys based on subgenus assignment
Start<-c("Thomomys_mazama", "Thomomys_monticola", "Thomomys_talpoides")
MIS<-c("Thomomys_clusius", "Thomomys_idahoensis")
MIS1<-MIS[sample.int(2, 1)]; SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS1); MIS<-MIS[MIS%in%MIS1==F]; Start<-c(Start, MIS1)
SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS)
#Place missing species of Orthogeomys based on subgenus assignment
Sister1( "Orthogeomys_grandis",  "Orthogeomys_cuniculus")

MIS1<-MIS[sample.int(2, 1)]; SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS1); MIS<-MIS[MIS%in%MIS1==F]; Start<-c(Start, MIS1)
SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS)
Sister1( "Orthogeomys_hispidus",  "Orthogeomys_lanius")

#Simulate potential branch lengths wihtin the family based on MRCA of family equal to 32.58 MYA based on Meredith et al (2011)
#A node called Rootnode_Geomyidae is temporarily added but will be deleted when the tree is combined with the remaining families in the order

#########################################################################Gliridae###############################################################################
################################################################################################################################################################

#One of the trees of the family from the posterior distribution
Gliridae<-read.tree(text="(((Graphiurus_ocularis:1,((Graphiurus_murinus:1,Graphiurus_kelleni:1):1,Graphiurus_microtis:1):1):1,Graphiurus_platyops:1):1,(((((Dryomys_nitedula:1,Dryomys_laniger:1):1,(Eliomys_quercinus:1,Eliomys_melanurus:1):1):1,Myomimus_roachi:1):1,Muscardinus_avellanarius:1):1,(Glirulus_japonicus:1,Glis_glis:1):1):1);")
#Temporarily add a taxon named B to handle placements near the root of the family tree
TR<-read.tree(text="(A:1, B:1);")
PHYLO<-Gliridae
PHYLO<<-bind.tree(TR , PHYLO,  1)
#One of the trees for the genus Graphiurus from the posterior distribution
Graphiurus<-read.tree(text="((Graphiurus_ocularis:1,(Graphiurus_microtis:1,((Graphiurus_kelleni:1,Graphiurus_lorraineus:1):1,Graphiurus_murinus:1):1):1):1,Graphiurus_platyops:1);")
MONOP.GROUP<-c("Graphiurus_kelleni", "Graphiurus_microtis", "Graphiurus_murinus", "Graphiurus_ocularis", "Graphiurus_platyops", "Graphiurus_lorraineus")
#Merging the family tree with the tree for Graphiurus
Replace.groups(Graphiurus, MONOP.GROUP)

#Place Dryomys_niethammeri based on taxonomy
SisterOrSing1(c("Dryomys_nitedula", "Dryomys_laniger"), "Dryomys_niethammeri")
#Place Chaetocauda as sister to Dryomys based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007)
SisterAnd1( c("Dryomys_nitedula", "Dryomys_laniger", "Dryomys_niethammeri"), "Chaetocauda_sichuanensis")
#Place missing species of Myomimus based on taxonomy
Sister2("Myomimus_roachi", "Myomimus_personatus", "Myomimus_setzeri")
#Place Selevinia as sister to Myomimus based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007)
SisterAnd1(c("Myomimus_roachi", "Myomimus_personatus", "Myomimus_setzeri"), "Selevinia_betpakdalaensis")
#Place Eliomys_munbyanus based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007)
Sister1("Eliomys_melanurus", "Eliomys_munbyanus")
#Place Eliomys_morpheus based on taxonomy
SisterOrSing1(c("Eliomys_melanurus", "Eliomys_munbyanus", "Eliomys_quercinus"), "Eliomys_morpheus")
#Place missing species of Graphiurus based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007)
Sister1("Graphiurus_kelleni", "Graphiurus_johnstoni")
Sister1("Graphiurus_platyops", "Graphiurus_angolensis")
Start<-c(list(c("Graphiurus_kelleni", "Graphiurus_johnstoni")), list(c("Graphiurus_platyops", "Graphiurus_angolensis")), "Graphiurus_lorraineus", "Graphiurus_microtis", "Graphiurus_murinus", "Graphiurus_ocularis")
MIS<-c("Graphiurus_christyi", "Graphiurus_monardi", "Graphiurus_rupicola", "Graphiurus_surdus")
MIS1<-MIS[sample.int(4, 1)]; SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS1); MIS<-MIS[MIS%in%MIS1==F]; Start<-c(Start, MIS1)
MIS1<-MIS[sample.int(3, 1)]; SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS1); MIS<-MIS[MIS%in%MIS1==F]; Start<-c(Start, MIS1)
MIS1<-MIS[sample.int(2, 1)]; SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS1); MIS<-MIS[MIS%in%MIS1==F]; Start<-c(Start, MIS1)
SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS)
SisterAnd1(c("Graphiurus_kelleni", "Graphiurus_johnstoni", "Graphiurus_platyops", "Graphiurus_angolensis", "Graphiurus_lorraineus", "Graphiurus_microtis", "Graphiurus_murinus", "Graphiurus_ocularis", "Graphiurus_christyi", "Graphiurus_monardi", "Graphiurus_rupicola", "Graphiurus_surdus"), "Graphiurus_crassicaudatus")
SisterAnd1(c("Graphiurus_kelleni", "Graphiurus_johnstoni", "Graphiurus_platyops", "Graphiurus_angolensis", "Graphiurus_lorraineus", "Graphiurus_microtis", "Graphiurus_murinus", "Graphiurus_ocularis", "Graphiurus_christyi", "Graphiurus_monardi", "Graphiurus_rupicola", "Graphiurus_surdus", "Graphiurus_crassicaudatus"), "Graphiurus_nagtglasii")
#Delete temporary taxon 
PHYLO<-drop.tip(PHYLO, "B")

#Simulate potential branch lengths wihtin the family based on MRCA of family equal to 30 MYA based on Meredith et al (2011)
BD.gen(30,0.685)
PHYLO->Gliridae

Start<-c("Gerbilliscus_guineae", "Gerbilliscus_robustus", "Gerbilliscus_afra", "Gerbilliscus_gambiana", "Gerbilliscus_kempi", "Gerbilliscus_leucogaster", "Gerbilliscus_nigricaudus", "Gerbilliscus_validus")
MIS<-c("Gerbilliscus_inclusus", "Gerbilliscus_phillipsi", "Gerbilliscus_boehmi")
MIS1<-MIS[sample.int(3, 1)]; SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS1); MIS<-MIS[MIS%in%MIS1==F]; Start<-c(Start, MIS1)
MIS1<-MIS[sample.int(2, 1)]; SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS1); MIS<-MIS[MIS%in%MIS1==F]; Start<-c(Start, MIS1)
SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS)

#Simulate potential branch lengths wihtin the family based on a divergence time with its closest relatives of 25.88 MYA following Meredith et al (2011)

################################################################################################################################################################
########################################################################Nesomyidae##############################################################################
################################################################################################################################################################

#One of the trees of the family from the posterior distribution
Nesomyidae<-read.tree(text="((((Monticolomys_koopmani:1,Macrotarsomys_bastardi:1):1,(((Brachyuromys_ramirohitra:1,Brachyuromys_betsileoensis:1):1,(Nesomys_audeberti:1,Nesomys_rufus:1):1):1,Hypogeomys_antimena:1):1):1,(Brachytarsomys_albicauda:1,(Gymnuromys_roberti:1,((Eliurus_antsingy:1,((((Eliurus_minor:1,Eliurus_myoxinus:1):1,Eliurus_webbi:1):1,Eliurus_tanala:1):1,Eliurus_majori:1):1):1,Voalavo_gymnocaudus:1):1):1):1):1,(((Saccostomus_campestris:1,((Dendromus_mystacalis:1,Malacothrix_typica:1):1,Steatomys_parvus:1):1):1,((Cricetomys_gambianus:1,Cricetomys_emini:1):1,Beamys_hindei:1):1):1,(Petromyscus_collinus:1,Mystromys_albicaudatus:1):1):1);")
PHYLO<-Nesomyidae
#One of the trees for the genus Eliurus from the posterior distribution
Eliurus<-read.tree(text="((((((Eliurus_webbi:1,Eliurus_ellermani:1):1,Eliurus_tanala:1):1,(Eliurus_myoxinus:1,Eliurus_minor:1):1):1,Eliurus_majori:1):1,Eliurus_antsingy:1):1,Eliurus_grandidieri:1);")
MONOP.GROUP<-c("Eliurus_antsingy", "Eliurus_majori", "Eliurus_minor", "Eliurus_myoxinus", "Eliurus_tanala", "Eliurus_webbi", "Eliurus_ellermani", "Eliurus_grandidieri")
#Merging the family tree with the tree for Eliurus
Replace.groups(Eliurus, MONOP.GROUP)

#Place Brachytarsomys_villosa based on taxonomy
Sister1("Brachytarsomys_albicauda", "Brachytarsomys_villosa")
#Place Dendroprionomys Megadendromus and Prionomys based on assumed monophyly of Dendromurinae
Rep_3_6("Dendromus_mystacalis", "Malacothrix_typica", "Steatomys_parvus", c("Dendroprionomys_rousseloti", "Megadendromus_nikolausi", "Prionomys_batesi"))
#Place missing species of Dendromus based on taxonomy
TR<-read.tree(text="(Dendromus_insignis:1, Dendromus_kahuziensis:1, Dendromus_kivu:1, Dendromus_lovati:1, Dendromus_melanotis:1, Dendromus_mesomelas:1, Dendromus_messorius:1, Dendromus_mystacalis:1, Dendromus_nyikae:1, Dendromus_oreas:1, Dendromus_vernayi:1):1;")
PHYLO<<-bind.tree(PHYLO, TR ,  getNode(phylo4(PHYLO),"Dendromus_mystacalis"))
#Place missing species of Petromyscus based on taxonomy
TR<-read.tree(text="(Petromyscus_barbouri:1,Petromyscus_collinus:1,Petromyscus_monticularis:1,Petromyscus_shortridgei:1):1;")
PHYLO<<-bind.tree(PHYLO, TR ,  getNode(phylo4(PHYLO),"Petromyscus_collinus"))
#Place Delanymys as sister to Petromyscus based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007).
SisterAnd1(c("Petromyscus_barbouri", "Petromyscus_collinus", "Petromyscus_monticularis", "Petromyscus_shortridgei"), "Delanymys_brooksi")
#Place missing species of Steatomys based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007)
TR<-read.tree(text="(Steatomys_caurinus:1, Steatomys_cuppedius:1, Steatomys_jacksoni:1,Steatomys_krebsii:1,Steatomys_parvus:1, Steatomys_pratensis:1):1:1;")
PHYLO<<-bind.tree(PHYLO, TR ,  getNode(phylo4(PHYLO),"Steatomys_parvus"))
Sister2("Steatomys_parvus", "Steatomys_bocagei", "Steatomys_opimus")
#Place missing species of Macrotarsomys based on taxonomy
Sister2("Macrotarsomys_bastardi", "Macrotarsomys_ingens", "Macrotarsomys_petteri")
#Place Nesomys_lambertoni based on taxonomy
SisterOrSing1(c("Nesomys_rufus", "Nesomys_audeberti"), "Nesomys_lambertoni")
#Place Saccostomus_mearnsi based on taxonomy
Sister1("Saccostomus_campestris", "Saccostomus_mearnsi")
#Place Voalavo_antsahabensis based on taxonomy
Sister1("Voalavo_gymnocaudus", "Voalavo_antsahabensis")
#Place missing species of Eliurus based on taxonomy
Start<-c("Eliurus_antsingy", "Eliurus_ellermani", "Eliurus_grandidieri", "Eliurus_majori", "Eliurus_minor", "Eliurus_myoxinus", "Eliurus_tanala", "Eliurus_webbi")
MIS<-c("Eliurus_danieli", "Eliurus_penicillatus", "Eliurus_petteri")
MIS1<-MIS[sample.int(3, 1)]; SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS1); MIS<-MIS[MIS%in%MIS1==F]; Start<-c(Start, MIS1)
MIS1<-MIS[sample.int(2, 1)]; SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS1); MIS<-MIS[MIS%in%MIS1==F]; Start<-c(Start, MIS1)
SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS)
#Place Hypogeomys_australis based on taxonomy
Sister1("Hypogeomys_antimena", "Hypogeomys_australis")

#Simulate potential branch lengths wihtin the family based on a divergence time with its closest relatives of 29.06 MYA following Meredith et al (2011)
#A node called Rootnode_Nesomyidae is temporarily added but will be deleted when the tree is combined with the remaining families in the order
PHYLO<-bind.tree(read.tree(text="(ROOT_1:1, Rootnode_Nesomyidae:1);"), PHYLO,1)
BD.gen(29.06,0.685)
PHYLO->Nesomyidae

#One of the trees of the family from the posterior distribution
Octodontidae<-read.tree(text="(((Tympanoctomys_barrerae:1,Pipanacoctomys_aureus:1):1,Octomys_mimax:1):1,((Spalacopus_cyanus:1,((Octodon_degus:1,(Octodon_lunatus:1,Octodon_bridgesi:1):1):1,(Aconaemys_porteri:1,(Aconaemys_sagei:1,Aconaemys_fuscus:1):1):1):1):1,Octodontomys_gliroides:1):1);")

#Place Octodon_pacificus based on taxonomy
SisterOrSing1(c("Octodon_bridgesi", "Octodon_degus", "Octodon_lunatus"), "Octodon_pacificus")
#Place Salinoctomys as sister to another genus in the family
SisterOrSing1(c(list(c("Aconaemys_fuscus", "Aconaemys_porteri", "Aconaemys_sagei")), list(c("Octodon_bridgesi", "Octodon_degus", "Octodon_lunatus", "Octodon_pacificus")), "Octodontomys_gliroides", "Octomys_mimax", "Pipanacoctomys_aureus", "Spalacopus_cyanus", "Tympanoctomys_barrerae"), "Salinoctomys_loschalchalerosorum")

PHYLO<-bind.tree(read.tree(text="(ROOT_1:1, Rootnode_Octodontidae:1);"), PHYLO,1)
YULE.gen(22.93)
PHYLO->Octodontidae

#One of the trees of the family from the posterior distribution
Spalacidae<-read.tree(text="((Spalax_ehrenbergi:1,(Tachyoryctes_splendens:1,Rhizomys_pruinosus:1):1):1,(Eospalax_smithii:1,Myospalax_aspalax:1):1);")
PHYLO<-Spalacidae
#Temporarily add a taxon named B to handle placements near the root of the family tree
TR<-read.tree(text="(A:1, B:1);")
PHYLO<<-bind.tree(TR , PHYLO,  1)
#One of the trees for the genus Eospalax from the posterior distribution
Eospalax<-read.tree(text="((Eospalax_fontanierii:1,Eospalax_smithii:1):1,Eospalax_rothschildi:1);")
MONOP.GROUP<-c("Eospalax_fontanierii", "Eospalax_rothschildi", "Eospalax_smithii")
#Merging the family tree with the tree for Eospalax
Replace.groups(Eospalax, MONOP.GROUP)
#One of the trees for the genus Spalax from the posterior distribution
Spalax<-read.tree(text="(((Spalax_ehrenbergi:1,Spalax_nehringi:1):1,Spalax_leucodon:1):1,((Spalax_zemni:1,Spalax_microphthalmus:1):1,Spalax_graecus:1):1);")
MONOP.GROUP<-c("Spalax_ehrenbergi", "Spalax_graecus", "Spalax_leucodon", "Spalax_microphthalmus", "Spalax_nehringi", "Spalax_zemni")
#Merging the family tree with the tree for Spalax
Replace.groups(Spalax, MONOP.GROUP)

#Place missing species of Myospalax based on taxonomy
Sister2("Myospalax_aspalax", "Myospalax_myospalax", "Myospalax_psilurus")
#Place missing species of Rhizomys based on taxonomy
Sister2("Rhizomys_pruinosus", "Rhizomys_sinensis", "Rhizomys_sumatrensis")
#Place Tachyoryctes_macrocephalus based on taxonomy
Sister1("Tachyoryctes_splendens", "Tachyoryctes_macrocephalus")
#Place Cannomys as sister to Rhizomys based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007)
SisterOrSing1(c("Rhizomys_pruinosus", "Rhizomys_sinensis", "Rhizomys_sumatrensis"), "Cannomys_badius")
#Place missing species of Spalax based on Nature 446, 507-512 (2007)
Start<-c("Spalax_graecus", "Spalax_microphthalmus", "Spalax_zemni")
MIS<-c("Spalax_arenarius", "Spalax_giganteus")
MIS1<-MIS[sample.int(2, 1)]; SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS1); MIS<-MIS[MIS%in%MIS1==F]; Start<-c(Start, MIS1)
SisterOrSing1(Start, MIS)
Sister1("Spalax_giganteus", "Spalax_uralensis")
#Delete temporary taxon 
PHYLO<-drop.tip(PHYLO, "B")

#Simulate potential branch lengths wihtin the family based on a divergence time with its closest relatives of 44.88 MYA following Meredith et al (2011)
#A node called Rootnode_Spalacidae is temporarily added but will be deleted when the tree is combined with the remaining families in the order
PHYLO<-bind.tree(read.tree(text="(ROOT_1:1, Rootnode_Spalacidae:1);"), PHYLO,1)
BD.gen(44.88,0.685)
PHYLO->Spalacidae

###########################################################The interfamily relationship#########################################################################
################################################################################################################################################################

#The relationsnip between the families in the order
#The relationship is not fully settled. A single tree is chosen here. The full set can be generated by sampling all trees with A4 varying betweemn 1 and 1000
A4<-sample.int(1000,1000)
if (A4[1]<929) {Rodents<-read.tree(text="((((Sciuridae:13.12, Aplodontia_rufa:49.12):11.37, Gliridae:30.49):6.87, (((((((((Myocastor_coypus:15.83,  Echimyidae:0):4.12, Capromyidae:0):6.7, (Octodontidae:0, Ctenomyidae:0):3.72):1.59, Abrocomidae:0):10.65, (Chinchillidae:0, Dinomys_branickii:28.19):10.7):3.08, (((Cavidae:10.59, Dasyproctidae:0):1.66, Cuniculidae:0):8.74, Erethizontidae:0):1.04):5.25, ((Petromus_typicus:26.16, Thyonomyidae:0):15.86, Bathyergidae:0):5.20):1.81, Hystricidae:21.53):11.98, (Ctenodactylidae:0, Laonastes_aenigmamus:43.13):17.88):6.35):1.6, ((((((((Muridae:0, Cricetidae:0):3.18, Nesomyidae:0):2.35, Calomyscidae:0):13.47,Spalacidae:0):4.67, Platacanthomyidae:0):4.67, Dipodidae:7.22):10.14, (Anomaluridae:11.79, (Pedetes_capensis:5, Pedetes_surdaster:5):46.79):12.57):0.74, ((Geomyidae:0, Heteromyidae:0):26.22, Castoridae:0):6.3):3.86);")} else
{Rodents<-read.tree(text="((((Sciuridae:13.12, Aplodontia_rufa:49.12):11.37, Gliridae:30.49):6.87, (((((((((Myocastor_coypus:15.83,  Echimyidae:0):4.12, Capromyidae:0):6.7, (Octodontidae:0, Ctenomyidae:0):3.72):1.59, Abrocomidae:0):10.65, (Chinchillidae:0, Dinomys_branickii:28.19):10.7):3.08, (((Cavidae:10.59, Dasyproctidae:0):1.66, Cuniculidae:0):8.74, Erethizontidae:0):1.04):5.25, ((Petromus_typicus:26.16, Thyonomyidae:0):15.86, Bathyergidae:0):5.20):1.81, Hystricidae:21.53):11.98, (Ctenodactylidae:0, Laonastes_aenigmamus:43.13):17.88):6.35):1.6, (((((((Muridae:0, Cricetidae:0):5.53, (Nesomyidae:0,  Calomyscidae:0):2.35):13.47,Spalacidae:0):4.67, Platacanthomyidae:0):4.67, Dipodidae:7.22):10.14, (Anomaluridae:11.79, (Pedetes_capensis:5, Pedetes_surdaster:5):46.79):12.57):0.74, ((Geomyidae:0, Heteromyidae:0):26.22, Castoridae:0):6.3):3.86);")}

#Adding the families one by one
Rodents<-bind.tree(Rodents, Abrocomidae, getNode(phylo4(Rodents),"Abrocomidae")); Rodents<-drop.tip(Rodents, "Rootnode_Abrocomidae")
Rodents<-bind.tree(Rodents, Anomaluridae, getNode(phylo4(Rodents),"Anomaluridae"))
Rodents<-bind.tree(Rodents, Bathyergidae, getNode(phylo4(Rodents),"Bathyergidae")); Rodents<-drop.tip(Rodents, "Rootnode_Bathyergidae")
if(A4[1]<929){Calomyscidae->PHYLO; BD.gen(31.41,0.685); Rodents<-bind.tree(Rodents, PHYLO, getNode(phylo4(Rodents),"Calomyscidae")); Rodents<-drop.tip(Rodents, "Rootnode_Calomyscidae")} else {Calomyscidae->PHYLO; BD.gen(29.06,0.685); Rodents<-bind.tree(Rodents, PHYLO, getNode(phylo4(Rodents),"Calomyscidae")); Rodents<-drop.tip(Rodents, "Rootnode_Calomyscidae")}
Rodents<-bind.tree(Rodents, Capromyidae, getNode(phylo4(Rodents),"Capromyidae")); Rodents<-drop.tip(Rodents, "Rootnode_Capromyidae")
Rodents<-bind.tree(Rodents, Castoridae, getNode(phylo4(Rodents),"Castoridae")); Rodents<-drop.tip(Rodents, "Rootnode_Castoridae")
